    (2): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
    (3): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=192, bias=True)
  )
  (msf_layers): ModuleList()
  (ccb_layers): ModuleList(
    (0): CCBLayer(
      (transformer_layer): CCB_TransformerLayer(
        (attention1): AttentionLayer(
          (q): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (k): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (v): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (attention): LinearAttention()
        )
        (attention2): AttentionLayer(
          (q): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (k): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (v): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (attention): LinearAttention()
        )
        (attention3): AttentionLayer(
          (q): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (k): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (v): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=192, bias=True)
          (attention): LinearAttention()
        )
        (MLP0): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=768, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=192, bias=True)
        )
        (MLP1): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=768, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=192, bias=True)
        )
        (MLP2): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=768, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=192, bias=True)
        )
        (MLP3): Sequential(
          (0): Linear(in_features=192, out_features=768, bias=True)
          (1): ReLU()
          (2): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=192, bias=True)
        )
        (norm0): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm11): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm12): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm21): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm22): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm31): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm32): LayerNorm((192,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm_xbg): LayerNorm((2, 192), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (base_merge): Conv1d(2, 1, kernel_size=(1,), stride=(1,), bias=False)
      )
      (cor_norm): LayerNorm((2, 192), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (semguid_norm): LayerNorm((2, 192), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
      (weight_mlp): Sequential(
        (0): Linear(in_features=384, out_features=384, bias=True)
        (1): LayerNorm((384,), eps=1e-05, elementwise_affine=True)
        (2): ReLU()
        (3): Dropout(p=0.1, inplace=False)
        (4): Linear(in_features=384, out_features=1, bias=True)
      )
    )
  )
  (class_reduce): MLPWithoutResidual(
    (fc1): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=3072, bias=True)
    (fc2): Linear(in_features=3072, out_features=192, bias=True)
    (relu): ReLU()
  )
  (bg_proto_reduce): MLPWithoutResidual(
    (fc1): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=400, bias=True)
    (fc2): Linear(in_features=400, out_features=100, bias=True)
    (relu): ReLU()
  )
  (IF_bg_proto_reduce): MLPWithoutResidual(
    (fc1): Linear(in_features=100, out_features=400, bias=True)
    (fc2): Linear(in_features=400, out_features=100, bias=True)
    (relu): ReLU()
  )
)
